  <section  class="container ns-asert">
    <div class="ns-flex__row ns-flex__row--wrap ns-flex__row--justify-between ns-flex__row--align-center">

                    <h1 class="heading ns-font--weight-extrabold ns-h2">Kardon Loader Looks for Beta Testers</h1>
                  </div>
        <div class="ns-col--m-s-12 ns-col--t-s-6 padding--right--none">
              <picture>
                  <source srcset="/sites/default/files/styles/container_wide_tablet/public/Kardon%20Loader%20Advertisement.png.webp?itok=-6okBk3n 1x, /sites/default/files/styles/container_wide_tablet_2x/public/Kardon%20Loader%20Advertisement.png.webp?itok=WAH4nDjM 2x" media="all and (min-width: 992px)" type="image/webp" width="1024" height="344"/>
              <source srcset="/sites/default/files/styles/container_wide_tabletsmall/public/Kardon%20Loader%20Advertisement.png.webp?itok=KTB-jbBq 1x, /sites/default/files/styles/container_wide_tabletsmall_2x/public/Kardon%20Loader%20Advertisement.png.webp?itok=fRBaYDHB 2x" media="all and (min-width: 768px)" type="image/webp" width="768" height="258"/>
              <source srcset="/sites/default/files/styles/container_wide_tabletsmall/public/Kardon%20Loader%20Advertisement.png.webp?itok=KTB-jbBq 1x, /sites/default/files/styles/container_wide_tabletsmall_2x/public/Kardon%20Loader%20Advertisement.png.webp?itok=fRBaYDHB 2x" media="all and (min-width: 480px)" type="image/webp" width="768" height="258"/>
              <source srcset="/sites/default/files/styles/container_wide_mobile/public/Kardon%20Loader%20Advertisement.png.webp?itok=MtrthH-W 1x, /sites/default/files/styles/container_wide_mobile_2x/public/Kardon%20Loader%20Advertisement.png.webp?itok=J6htXB2v 2x" media="all and (min-width: 320px)" type="image/webp" width="480" height="161"/>
                  <img loading="eager" width="960" height="540" src="/sites/default/files/styles/two_column_lazy_load/public/Kardon%20Loader%20Advertisement.png.webp?itok=b2cySXHY" alt="Kardon Loader Advertisement" />

  </picture>


        </div>
      
    </div>

    <div class="padding--top--md ns-flex__row--basic ns-flex__row--wrap ns-flex__row--align-center">
              <span class="margin--right--xsml">by </span>
        <span  class="margin--right--xsml margin--bottom--none"><a href="https://www.netscout.com/blog/asert/asert-team"  class="link link--darkteal"><span about="https://www.netscout.com/blog/asert/asert-team" typeof="schema:Person" property="schema:name" datatype="">ASERT Team</span></a></span>

        <span class="margin--right--xsml">on </span>
            <time class="ns-font--transform-upper ns-font--weight-bold">June 19th, 2018</time>
    </div>
    <div class="some-sharing-links padding--top--xsml padding--bottom--md ns-container--b-bottom">
      <span class="a2a_kit a2a_kit_size_32 addtoany_list" data-a2a-url="https://www.netscout.com/blog/asert/kardon-loader-looks-beta-testers" data-a2a-title="Kardon Loader Looks for Beta Testers"><a class="a2a_button_linkedin"></a><a class="a2a_button_x"></a><a class="a2a_button_facebook"></a><a class="a2a_button_copy_link"></a><a class="a2a_dd addtoany_share" href="https://www.addtoany.com/share#url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.netscout.com%2Fblog%2Fasert%2Fkardon-loader-looks-beta-testers&amp;title=Kardon%20Loader%20Looks%20for%20Beta%20Testers"></a></span>

    </div>
    <div class="wysiwyg margin--top-bottom--lg ns-font--overflow-break-word ns-font--overflow-hidden">
      <div class="has-datatables">
      <h2>Key Findings</h2><ul><li>ASERT researchers discovered Kardon Loader being advertised on underground forums.</li><li>Kardon Loader features functionality allowing customers to open their own botshop, which grants the purchaser the ability to rebuild the bot and sell access to others.</li><li>Kardon Loader is in early stages of development, public beta.</li><li>Incorporates numerous anti-analysis checks to discourage analysis.</li></ul><h2>Executive Summary</h2><p>Kardon&nbsp;Loader is a malware downloader&nbsp;advertised on underground forums as a paid open beta product. This malware has been on sale by an actor under the username&nbsp;Yattaze, starting in late April.&nbsp;The actor offers the sale of the malware as a standalone build&nbsp;with charges for each additional rebuild, or the ability to set up a&nbsp;botshop&nbsp;in which case any customer can establish their own operation and&nbsp;further sell access to a new customer base.</p><p>Malware authors and distributors leverage downloader malware and&nbsp;botshops&nbsp;to build malware distribution networks.&nbsp;Malware distribution networks are commonly used by cyber criminals to create botnets&nbsp;to&nbsp;distribute&nbsp;additional payloads such as credential theft malware,&nbsp;ransomware, banking Trojans, and others. These distribution networks are often run by&nbsp;third party operators and offered as a service in underground markets.</p><p><strong>NOTE:&nbsp;ASERT actively&nbsp;collects indicators associated with this malware family to provide protection for our&nbsp;Netscout&nbsp;Arbor customers.&nbsp;</strong></p><h2>History</h2><p>On April&nbsp;21, 2018&nbsp;actor&nbsp;Yattaze&nbsp;began advertising the open public beta of a&nbsp;downloader&nbsp;named&nbsp;Kardon&nbsp;Loader for $50. The description of the malware family suggests this malware was&nbsp;a&nbsp;rebrand of the&nbsp;ZeroCool&nbsp;botnet which was under development previously by the same actor.&nbsp;The actor has&nbsp;had an account&nbsp;on the forum since April 2017 and received multiple vouches for this product.&nbsp;The advertisement for the loader is&nbsp;professional looking with its own logo&nbsp;(<strong>Figure 1</strong>&nbsp;&amp;&nbsp;<strong>Figure 2</strong>).&nbsp;</p><p><span class="TextRun SCXW105957596" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW105957596"><img alt="Kardon Loader Advertisement" data-entity-type="file" data-entity-uuid="ea3f43eb-90cb-442e-b7ac-0a814dadf725" src="/sites/default/files/inline-images/Kardon%20Loader%20Advertisement.png" width="1024" height="344" loading="lazy"></span></span></p><p><span class="TextRun SCXW105957596" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW105957596">Figure 1: The advertisement for the loader is&nbsp;</span></span><span class="TextRun SCXW105957596" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW105957596">professional looking with its own logo.</span></span></p><p><a href="https://www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_pricing.png"><img alt="Kardon Loader Pricing" class="size-large wp-image-9579" height="1024" src="//www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_pricing-708x1024.png" width="708" loading="lazy"></a> Figure 2: Kardon Loader Pricing[/caption] <span class="TextRun SCXW72313799" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW72313799">The actor provides a disclaimer stating this software should not be used for malicious purposes</span></span><span class="TextRun SCXW72313799" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW72313799">&nbsp;(</span></span><strong><span class="TextRun SCXW72313799" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW72313799">Figure 3</span></span></strong><span class="TextRun SCXW72313799" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW72313799">)</span></span><span class="TextRun SCXW72313799" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW72313799">.</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW72313799">&nbsp;</span>&nbsp;</p><p><a href="https://www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_disclaimer.png"><img alt="Kardon Loader Disclaimer" class="size-large wp-image-9575" height="199" src="//www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_disclaimer-1024x226.png" width="900" loading="lazy"></a> Figure 3: Kardon Loader Disclaimer[/caption] <span class="TextRun SCXW258453631" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW258453631">Additionally, the actor uploaded a YouTube video showing the panel functionality from an admin standpoint</span></span><span class="TextRun SCXW258453631" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW258453631">&nbsp;(</span></span><strong><span class="TextRun SCXW258453631" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW258453631">Figure 4</span></span></strong><span class="TextRun SCXW258453631" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW258453631">)</span></span><span class="TextRun SCXW258453631" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW258453631">.</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW258453631">&nbsp;</span></p><p><a href="//www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_youtube.png"><img alt="Kardon Loader YouTube Walkthrough" class="size-full wp-image-9580" height="274" src="//www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_youtube.png" width="460" loading="lazy"></a> Figure 4: Kardon Loader YouTube Walkthrough&nbsp;</p><h2>Distribution</h2><p>Insights gained from the forum thread&nbsp;suggest the actor initially conducted tests by leveraging a well-known&nbsp;botshop&nbsp;named&nbsp;Pink Panthers automated loads shop&nbsp;(Pink).&nbsp;Commentary from the actor reveals this bot is not widely distributed at this time.&nbsp;Only 124 infections are shown in a screenshot of the loaders test network&nbsp;posted by the actor&nbsp;(<strong>Figure 5</strong>).</p><p><a href="https://www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_dashmap.png"><img alt="Kardon Loader Administrator Panel Showing Infections" class="size-large wp-image-9574" height="665" src="//www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_dashmap-1024x757.png" width="900" loading="lazy"></a> Figure 5: Kardon Loader Administrator Panel Showing Infections[/caption]</p><h2>Analysis</h2><p>The actor alleges the following functionality is available or forthcoming to&nbsp;Kardon&nbsp;Loader:</p><ul><li>Bot Functionality</li><li>Download and Execute Task</li><li>Update Task</li><li>Uninstall Task</li><li>Usermode&nbsp;Rootkit</li><li>RC4 Encryption (Not Yet Implemented)</li><li>Debug and Analysis Protection</li><li>TOR Support</li><li>Domain Generation Algorithm&nbsp;(DGA)</li></ul><p>ASERT&nbsp;found&nbsp;many of these features&nbsp;absent&nbsp;in the samples reviewed. All samples analyzed used hard-coded command and control&nbsp;(C2)&nbsp;URLs instead of DGA. There was also no evidence of&nbsp;TOR&nbsp;or user mode rootkit&nbsp;functionality&nbsp;in the binaries.</p><h2>Anti-Analysis Techniques</h2><p>Kardon&nbsp;Loader uses&nbsp;a few anti-analysis techniques,&nbsp;such as attempting to get the module handle for the following DLLs:</p><ul><li>avghookx.dll</li><li>avghooka.dll</li><li>snxhk.dll</li><li>sbiedll.dll</li><li>dbghelp.dll</li><li>api_log.dll</li><li>dir_watch.dll</li><li>pstorec.dll</li><li>vmcheck.dll</li><li>wpespy.dll</li></ul><p>If any of the above DLL handles are returned it will exit the process. These DLLs are associated with antivirus, analysis&nbsp;tools,&nbsp;and virtualization.&nbsp;Kardon&nbsp;Loader will also enumerate the CPUID Vendor ID value and compare it against the following strings:</p><ul><li>KVMKVMKVM</li><li>Microsoft&nbsp;Hv</li><li>VMwareVMware</li><li>XenVMMXenVMM</li><li>prl&nbsp;hyperv</li><li>VBoxVBoxVBox</li></ul><p>These are known CPUID Vendor ID values associated with virtualized machines.&nbsp;If one of these values are detected the&nbsp;malware&nbsp;will also exit.</p><h2>Command and Control</h2><p>Kardon&nbsp;Loader&nbsp;uses&nbsp;HTTP based&nbsp;C2&nbsp;infrastructure with URL&nbsp;parameters that are base64 encoded. Upon execution&nbsp;Kardon&nbsp;Loader will send&nbsp;HTTP POSTs&nbsp;to the C2 with the following fields:</p><ul><li><strong>ID</strong> = Identification Number</li><li><strong>OS</strong> = Operating System</li><li><strong>PV</strong> = User Privilege</li><li><strong>IP</strong> = Initial Payload (Full Path)</li><li><strong>CN</strong> = Computer Name</li><li><strong>UN</strong> = User Name</li><li><strong>CA</strong> = Processor Architecture</li></ul><p>An example of the POST payload sent from&nbsp;Kardon&nbsp;Loader sample upon execution&nbsp;can be seen in (<b>Figure 6</b>): [caption id="attachment_9578" align="aligncenter" width="900"]<a href="https://www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_pcap.png"><img alt="Kardon Loader POST Request" class="size-large wp-image-9578" height="182" src="//www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_pcap-1024x207.png" width="900" loading="lazy"></a> Figure 6: Kardon Loader POST Request[/caption] Once the request is made,&nbsp;the&nbsp;C2 server will provide varying&nbsp;feedback which will result in&nbsp;either&nbsp;downloading and executing additional payloads, visiting a website, upgrading current payloads,&nbsp;or uninstalling&nbsp;itself. The C2 server response format for a wait command is:</p><ul><li><strong>notask</strong></li></ul><p>While other commands including the download and execution functionality use&nbsp;the following format:</p><ul><li><strong>newtask`##`#&nbsp;&lt;url&gt;&nbsp;</strong><ul><li>Hashmarks represent the&nbsp;two-character task&nbsp;id and&nbsp;one-character&nbsp;task&nbsp;value</li></ul></li></ul><p>Next,&nbsp;the infected host will send a confirmation message back to the C2 in the same format as the initial post payload with&nbsp;the following&nbsp;additional fields:</p><ul><li><strong>TD</strong> =&nbsp;Task&nbsp;Identifier&nbsp;(Provided by&nbsp;command and control)</li><li><strong>OP</strong> =&nbsp;Task Output (1 if successful, 2 if not successful)</li></ul><p>Analysis of various samples reveal another parameter used for uninstalling of the loader directed by the&nbsp;C2:</p><ul><li><strong>UN</strong> =&nbsp;Uninstalled</li></ul><p>Posts from the actor on their advertisement thread suggests&nbsp;that C2 communication for this family will be changed to RC4 encryption in the future.&nbsp;Also, if the actor truly implements DGA, it may use it as a fallback mechanism for C2.</p><h2>Administration Panel</h2><p><br><a href="https://www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_panel1.png"><img alt="Kardon Loader Admin Panel" class="size-large wp-image-9576" height="450" src="//www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_panel1-1024x512.png" width="900" loading="lazy"></a> The panel for&nbsp;Kardon&nbsp;Loader incorporates a simple design with a dashboard of the bot distribution and install statistics. A notable feature of this panel is the bot store functionality allowing the bot admin to&nbsp;generate access keys to customers that would give them the ability to execute tasks based on the predefined parameters&nbsp;(<strong>Figure 8</strong>).</p><p><a href="https://www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_panel2.png"><img alt="Kardon Loader Store" class="size-large wp-image-9577" height="452" src="//www.netscout.com/sites/default/files/asert-blog/uploads/2018/06/kardon_panel2-1024x514.png" width="900" loading="lazy"></a> Figure 8: Kardon Loader Store[/caption] <span class="TextRun SCXW69772349" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW69772349">Users can specify a URL then provide the task type and number of executions in order to distribute commands to bots on the network.&nbsp;</span></span><span class="TextRun SCXW69772349" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW69772349">This is shown in the actors instructional YouTube video</span></span><span class="TextRun SCXW69772349" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW69772349">&nbsp;(</span></span><strong><span class="TextRun SCXW69772349" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW69772349">Figure 4</span></span></strong><span class="TextRun SCXW69772349" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW69772349">)</span></span><span class="TextRun SCXW69772349" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW69772349">.</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW69772349">&nbsp;</span></p><h2>Conclusion and Recommendations</h2><p>This article is an overview of the downloader malware known as&nbsp;Kardon&nbsp;Loader.&nbsp;Kardon&nbsp;Loader is a fully featured downloader, enabling the download and installation of other malware,&nbsp;eg. banking trojans/credential theft etc. Downloaders are a critical part of the malware ecosystem, often developed by specialists and sold&nbsp;independently&nbsp;of the trojan that is the objective of the campaign. Although only in public beta stage this malware features bot store functionality allowing purchasers to&nbsp;open up&nbsp;their own&nbsp;botshop&nbsp;with this platform.&nbsp;The actor started advertising this loader in late April and has communicated further development will do done on this loader in the future,&nbsp;including encrypted C2 communications.</p><p>At a minimum organizations should leverage the indicators contained within this report to block malicious activity associated with&nbsp;Kardon&nbsp;Loader.&nbsp;Researchers may also leverage the Yara rule below to look for additional copies of&nbsp;Kardon&nbsp;Loader&nbsp;to&nbsp;extract other IOCs for blocking malicious activity.</p><h3>Yara Rule</h3><ul><li><a href="https://gist.github.com/arbor-asert/2ad9c7d715f41efc9d59ed8c425d10d3">https://gist.github.com/arbor-asert/2ad9c7d715f41efc9d59ed8c425d10d3</a></li></ul><h3>Hashes</h3><ul><li><span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW81600825" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW81600825">fd0dfb173aff74429c6fed55608ee99a24e28f64ae600945e15bf5fce6406aee</span></span></li><li><span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW28929297" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW28929297">b1a1deaacec7c8ac43b3dad8888640ed77b2a4d44f661a9e52d557e7833c7a21</span></span></li><li><span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW95472926" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW95472926">3c64d7dbef4b7e0dd81a5076172451334fe9669800c40c895567226f7cb7cdc7</span></span></li></ul><h3>Command and Control URLs</h3><ul><li>Kardon[.]ddns[.]net</li><li>Jhuynfrkijucdxiu[.]club</li><li>Kreuzberg[.]ru</li><li>Cryptdrop[.]xyz</li></ul>      </div>
    </div>
